# Lexemes

_This is an automatically generated documentation based on omorfi lexical database._

Lexemes are the word-entries of omorfi, currently we have only documented the ones that are commonly problematic, in terms of unexpected ambiguity, exceptional spelling or anything otherwise worth noting.

In attributes column we use following emoji shorthands:
* â˜¢ for lexemes listed as unlikely for disambiguation purposes
* ğŸ§‘Â¹ for first name of a person
* â™‚ for primarily male names
* â™€ for primarily female names
* ğŸ§‘Â² for surname of a person
* ğŸŒ for geographic location
* âš for a country
* ğŸ’± for currencies
* ğŸ“º for media
* ğŸ¶ for band or artists
* ğŸ—ª for languages
* org for organisations
* ğŸ“ for unit of measurement
* â° for point in time or span of time
* âˆ for proper noun not suitable for other categories of proper nouns

We link to all original sources for reference.
